            function getQueryVariable(variable) {
              var query = window.location.search.substring(1);
              var vars = query.split("&");
              for (var i = 0; i < vars.length; i++) {
                var pair = vars[i].split("=");
                if (pair[0] == variable) {
                  return pair[1];
                }
              }
              return (false);
            }

/*------------------------------------*\
  #Import
\*------------------------------------*/
/**
 * Use Objects to Name Different Colours.
 *
 * While maintaining colour variables,
 * one thing been found really painful is naming new colours.
 *
 * For example, if we need to add a new grey colour which is for menu background,
 * usually it would be named as `menuBackgroundGrey` straightforwardly,
 * but what if this grey is also for the text color?
 * Then we will see this:
 *
 * `color: $menuBackgroundGrey;` or `background-color: $naviTextGrey`
 *
 * It does look bit weird, but I think this is still fine,
 * what really painful is there are always multiple menus existing in website.
 * so we need to add more adjective words to separate them.
 *
 * `$menuBackgroundGreyLight`, `$menuBackgroundGreyDark` ...
 *
 * In that way, we just hope we wouldn't have more grey variables
 * when available vocabularies is about to running out.
 *
 * THEREFORE, I've decided to add a new naming convention to maintain colours variables,
 * which is `naming new colours by Objects`.
 *
 * TODO: Progressively immigrating to naming colours in Objects.
 *   In that approach, we should manage variables naming with less pain.
 *
 */
/*------------------------------------*\
  #Grey (by Animals)
\*------------------------------------*/
/*------------------------------------*\
  #Red (by Fruit)
\*------------------------------------*/
/*------------------------------------*\
  #Blue (by Bottled Water Brands)
\*------------------------------------*/
/*------------------------------------*\
  #Green (by Plants)
\*------------------------------------*/
/*------------------------------------*\
  #Yellow (by Fruit)
\*------------------------------------*/
/*------------------------------------*\
  #Orange (by Fruit)
\*------------------------------------*/
/*------------------------------------*\
  #Literal
\*------------------------------------*/
/*------------------------------------*\
  #Bookmakers Colours
\*------------------------------------*/
/*------------------------------------*\
  #Padding and Margins
\*------------------------------------*/
/*------------------------------------*\
  #Generic
\*------------------------------------*/
/*------------------------------------*\
  #Font family
\*------------------------------------*/
/*------------------------------------*\
  #Font Weight
\*------------------------------------*/

\*------------------------------------*/
